style="width:0.1%"></td><td style="width:1.0%"></td><td style="width:74.924%"></td><td style="width:0.1%"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="3" style="padding:0 1pt"><div><img alt="nflxlogo2015a22a.jpg" src="nflxlogo2015a22a.jpg" style="height:22px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:86px"></div></td><td colspan="3" style="padding:2px 1pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:top"><div style="text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">1</font></div></td></tr></table></div></div></div><div id="i7f52a9ace1f14334bfdd5fde2069c96b_4"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:63pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Q2 Results</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Revenue grew 17% in Q2 (or 22% on a foreign exchange (F&#47;X) neutral basis)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">2</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">, driven primarily by a 16% year over year increase in average paid memberships. ARM</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">3</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> was up 1% year over year or 5% on a F&#47;X neutral basis. Similar to recent quarters, the primary difference between F&#47;X neutral and reported growth was large peso price increases in Argentina due to local inflation and the devaluation of the Argentine peso relative to the US dollar. Global revenue was 1% higher than our beginning of quarter guidance due primarily to stronger-than-forecasted paid net additions of 8.0M vs. 5.9M in Q2&#8217;23. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Operating income for Q2 amounted to $2.6B, an increase of 42% vs. Q2&#8217;23. Operating margin of 27.2% improved five percentage points vs. 22.3% in the year ago quarter. Both were slightly above our guidance forecast due to higher than expected revenue. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Q2&#8217;24 EPS was $4.88  vs. $3.29 (+48% year over year). Net income included a $43 million non-cash unrealized gain from F&#47;X remeasurement on our Euro denominated debt, which is recognized below operating income in &#8220;interest and other income.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Forecast</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">As a reminder, the quarterly guidance we provide is our actual internal forecast at the time we report. Our primary financial metrics are revenue for growth and operating margin for profitability. Our goals are to sustain healthy revenue growth, expand our operating margin and grow free cash flow.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">For Q3&#8217;24, we expect revenue growth of 14% year over year. On a F&#47;X neutral basis this translates into 19% revenue growth due primarily to the price changes in Argentina and the devaluation of the local currency relative to the US dollar. We expect paid net additions to be lower than Q3&#8217;23, which had the first full quarter impact from paid sharing. Like recent quarters, we forecast global ARM on a reported basis to be roughly flat year over year in Q3 due to ongoing F&#47;X headwinds and plan and country mix. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">For the full year 2024, based on F&#47;X rates at the end of Q2&#8217;24, we now expect revenue growth of 14% to 15%, up from 13% to 15% previously. Our updated revenue forecast reflects solid membership growth trends and business momentum, partially offset by the strengthening of the US dollar vs. most other currencies. We also now expect 2024 operating margin of 26% based on F&#47;X rates as of January 1, 2024, up from our prior estimate of 25%, due to the improved revenue outlook and ongoing expense discipline. As we&#8217;ve noted in the past, while we've launched a F&#47;X risk management program to reduce near term volatility, we don&#8217;t intend to be fully hedged, which is why we guide and manage to a F&#47;X neutral operating margin target. Our goal is to increase our operating margin each year, though the rate of expansion will vary year to year.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Engagement &#38; Competition</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Viewing is key to Netflix&#8217;s success. It&#8217;s the best proxy we have for member happiness, and when people watch more, they stick around longer (retention), talk about Netflix more often (which drives acquisition) and place a higher value on our service. According to Nielsen, streaming accounts for 40% of total TV time in the US today, with Netflix and YouTube the clear leaders in direct to consumer</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">__________________________________</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">2</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> Excluding the year over year effect of foreign exchange rate movements and the impact of hedging gains&#47;losses realized as revenues. Assumes foreign exchange rates remained constant with foreign exchange rates from each of the corresponding months of the prior-year period.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">3 </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">ARM (Average Revenue per Membership) is defined as streaming revenue divided by the average number of streaming paid memberships divided by the number of months in the period. These figures do not include sales taxes or VAT.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:63pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><table style="border-collapse:collapse;display:inline-table;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:100.000%"><tr><td style="width:1.0%"></td><td style="width:25.182%"></td><td style="width:0.1%"></td><td style="width:1.0%"></td><td style="width:72.618%"></td><td style="width:0.1%"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="3" style="padding:0 1pt"><div><img alt="nflxlogo2015a22a.jpg" src="nflxlogo2015a22a.jpg" style="height:22px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:86px"></div></td><td colspan="3" style="padding:2px 1pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:top"><div style="text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">2</font></div></td></tr></table></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:63pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">entertainment. Collectively our two services account for almost half of all streaming TV watch time in the US. In H1 2024 (and despite headwinds from paid sharing) Netflix generated more view hours in the Nielsen Top 10 across film, series and licensed titles than all the other streamers combined. The challenge for so many of our competitors is that while they are investing heavily in premium content, it&#8217;s generating relatively small viewing on their streaming services and linear continues to decline.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><img alt="q2nielsengraph.jpg" src="q2nielsengraph.jpg" style="height:333px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:565px"></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Netflix and YouTube compete for people&#8217;s time and attention. Our movies and TV shows drive excitement and fan engagement on YouTube, as well as social media. We believe that our entertainment offering satisfies important needs for both consumers and the creators of great movies and TV shows, who need partners that can share in the risk inherent in bringing these stories to life. So looking to the future, we believe our biggest opportunity is winning a larger share of the 80%+ of TV time (primarily linear and streaming) that neither Netflix nor YouTube has today. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">If we execute well &#8212; better stories, easier discovery and more fandom &#8212; while also establishing ourselves in newer areas like live, games and advertising, we believe that we have a lot more room to grow. Across streaming, pay TV, film, games and branded advertising, it&#8217;s a $600B+ market, and today Netflix accounts for just &#126;6% of that revenue. But success starts with the consumer. Because when we delight people with our entertainment, Netflix can drive higher engagement, revenue and profit than the competition. This in turn creates a more loved and valued entertainment company &#8212; for our members, creators and shareholders &#8212; that we can strengthen and grow over time.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Improving our Entertainment Offering</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">As we explained in the latest version of our </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">culture memo</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">4</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">, which we published in June, &#8220;Netflix has come a long way since we mailed our first DVD in 1998. style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:111%;text-decoration:underline">Netflix Top 10</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:111%">.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:111%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">7</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">7</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> https&#58;&#47;&#47;www.netflix.com&#47;tudum&#47;top10&#47;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> https&#58;&#47;&#47;www.netflix.com&#47;tudum&#47;articles&#47;nfl-games-on-netflix</font></div><div style="height:63pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><table style="border-collapse:collapse;display:inline-table;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:100.000%"><tr><td style="width:1.0%"></td><td style="width:25.182%"></td><td style="width:0.1%"></td><td style="width:1.0%"></td><td style="width:72.618%"></td><td style="width:0.1%"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="3" style="padding:0 1pt"><div><img alt="nflxlogo2015a22a.jpg" src="nflxlogo2015a22a.jpg" style="height:22px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:86px"></div></td><td colspan="3" style="padding:2px 1pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:top"><div style="text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">4</font></div></td></tr></table></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:63pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Netflix IP are very appealing too, especially when timed to the launch of a series or film. In September 2023, we launched Netflix Stories &#8212; an ever increasing catalog of interactive fiction games based on hit Netflix series and films &#8211; with </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Love is Blind</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">. In Q2, we added </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Virgin River</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> and </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Perfect Match</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">. Starting in July we&#8217;ll launch about one new title per month like </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Emily in Paris</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> and </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Selling Sunset</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">. Separately, we will premiere a multiplayer game based on the </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Squid Game</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> universe later this year timed to the launch of season two of our biggest TV series ever.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Product</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">With so many titles &#8212; plus now games and live &#8212; it&#8217;s imperative that members can easily find the right title or game at the right moment. While our recommendations are widely recognized as industry leading, we believe we can do much more to improve discovery on Netflix. So we recently began testing a new, more intuitive TV homepage design, our biggest update in a decade. This new interface provides more visible title information at a glance &#8212; including synopsis, genre and ratings. Title previews are also larger and more dynamic, with more immersive trailers and bigger box art to make browsing easier. We&#8217;ve also simplified the navigation bar and moved it to the top of the page to create quicker, easier short cuts. And this new design includes My Netflix, which has everything members have saved or watched and was previously only available on mobile. As always with any changes to our product, we&#8217;ll listen to the feedback, learn and continue to improve the experience over time.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Partnerships</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">From the early days of streaming, we saw partnerships with device makers and pay TV and mobile operators as key to ensuring Netflix was easy to find and use. These partnerships are a win-win &#8212; making it simple for people to discover, sign-up, use and pay for Netflix. In turn, our device and operator partners benefit through increased device sales from consumers seeking devices integrated with Netflix and greater customer acquisition and higher retention as well as the opportunity to upsell higher value data or content packages. We haven&#8217;t bundled Netflix solely with other streamers like </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">Disney+ or Max</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">9</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> because Netflix already operates as a go-to destination for entertainment thanks to the breadth and variety of our slate and superior product experience. This has driven industry leading penetration, engagement and retention for us, which limits the benefit to Netflix of bundling directly with other streamers</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">10</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">.  </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Advertising</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Ads fulfill two important strategic priorities for Netflix&#58; first they enable us to offer lower prices to consumers&#59; and second, they create an additional revenue and profit stream for the business. Just over 18 months since launch, we continue to scale our ads tier, which now accounts for over 45% of all signups in our ads markets. Its attractiveness ($6.99 a month in the US, with two streams, high definition and downloads) &#8212; coupled with the phasing out of our Basic plan in the UK and Canada, which we will now start in the US and France &#8212; has increased our ads member base by 34% sequentially in Q2.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">We also continue to improve the service we offer advertisers. For example, in the UK, starting September, Barb will measure Netflix&#8217;s ad supported plan, making it easier for clients to plan campaigns and understand their audiences on Netflix. We also have new features like the &#8220;pause&#8221; or &#8220;keep watching&#8221; ads and in the two months since the launch of the beta in May, we&#8217;ve closed over 60 pause ad campaigns with big brands like Expedia, Coca-Cola, Ford, L'Or&#233;al  and McDonald&#8217;s. Most important of all, at our Upfront, we announced our new, in-house ad tech platform, which we&#8217;ll test in Canada later in 2024 and launch more broadly in 2025. This will give advertisers new ways to buy, insights to leverage </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">___________________________________</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">9</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> https&#58;&#47;&#47;press.disneyplus.com&#47;disney-entertainment-and-warner-bros-discovery-announce-disney-plus-hulu-max-bundle</font></div><div><font style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:63pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">and ways to measure impact. On the programmatic side, we&#8217;ll also expand our capabilities this summer to include The Trade Desk, Google DV 360, and Magnite.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Given this sustained progress, we believe that we&#8217;re on track to achieve critical ad subscriber scale for advertisers in our ad countries in 2025, creating a strong base from which we can further increase our ad membership in 2026 and beyond. Our ad revenue is growing nicely and is becoming a more meaningful contributor to our business. But building a business from scratch takes time &#8212; and coupled with the large size of our subscription revenue &#8212; we don't expect advertising to be a primary driver of our revenue growth in 2024 or 2025. The near term challenge (and medium term opportunity) is that we&#8217;re scaling faster than our ability to monetize our growing ad inventory. It&#8217;s why continuing to build our ad sales, measurement and tech capabilities is so important. Based on everything we&#8217;ve learned and our progress over the last 18 months &#8212; we&#8217;re confident that advertising will be a key component of our longer term revenue and profit growth.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Cash Flow and Capital Structure</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Net cash generated by operating activities in Q2 was $1.3B vs. $1.4 billion in the prior year period. Free cash flow(FCF)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">11</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> totaled $1.2B compared with $1.3B in last year&#8217;s Q2. We continue to expect full year 2024 FCF of approximately $6B, assuming no material swings in F&#47;X rates. During Q2, we repurchased 2.6M shares for $1.6B and we have $5B remaining under our existing authorization. At quarter end, gross debt totaled $14B, while cash, cash equivalents, and short-term investments amounted to $6.7B. We have $1.8B of debt maturities in the next twelve months, which we plan to refinance.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG)</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">We recently published our fifth annual Environmental, Social and Governance (ESG) </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">report</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">12</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">. </font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">here</font><font executive pay.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#666666;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Use of Non-GAAP Measures</font></div><div><font style="color:#222222;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">This shareholder letter and its attachments include reference to the non-GAAP financial measures of F&#47;X neutral revenue and adjusted operating profit and margin, and free cash flow. Management believes that free cash flow is an important liquidity metric because it measures, during a given period, the amount of cash generated that is available to repay debt obligations, make strategic acquisitions and investments and for certain other activities like stock repurchases. Management believes that F&#47;X neutral revenue and adjusted operating profit and margin allow investors to compare our projected results to our actual results absent year-over-year and intra-year currency fluctuations, respectively, and the impact of restructuring costs. However, these non-GAAP financial measures should be considered in addition to, not as a substitute for or superior to, net income, operating income (profit), operating margin, diluted earnings per share and net cash provided by (used in) operating activities, or other financial measures prepared in accordance with GAAP. Reconciliation to the GAAP equivalent of these non-GAAP measures are contained in tabular form on the attached unaudited financial statements and in the F&#47;X neutral operating margin disclosure above. We are not able to reconcile forward-looking non-GAAP financial measures because we are unable to predict without unreasonable effort the exact amount or timing of the reconciling items, including property and equipment and change in other assets, and the impact of changes in currency exchange rates. The variability of these items could have a significant impact on our future GAAP financial results.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#666666;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div><font style="color:#222222;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">This shareholder letter contains certain forward-looking statements within the meaning of the federal securities laws, including statements regarding our expected results for the fiscal quarter ending September 30, 2024 and fiscal year ending December 31, 2024&#59; adoption and growth of streaming entertainment&#59; growth strategy and outlook&#59; market opportunity&#59; competitive landscape and position&#59; entertainment offerings, including TV shows, movies, games, and live programming&#59; engagement&#59; slate strength&#59; pricing and plans strategy&#59; ad-supported tier and its prospects&#59; ads business&#59; product strategy&#59; partnerships&#59; impact of foreign exchange rates&#59; foreign currency exchange hedging program&#59;  stock repurchases&#59; debt refinancings&#59; paid net additions&#59; revenue and revenue growth&#59; ARM, operating income, operating margin, net income, earnings per share, and free cash flow. The forward-looking statements in this letter are subject to risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results and events to differ, including, without limitation&#58; our ability to attract new members and retain existing members&#59; our ability to compete effectively, including for consumer engagement with different modes of entertainment&#59; failing to improve the variety and quality of entertainment offerings&#59; adoption of the ads plan and paid sharing&#59; maintenance and expansion of device platforms for streaming&#59; fluctuations in consumer usage of our service&#59; service disruptions&#59; production risks&#59; macroeconomic conditions and timing of content releases.
